<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впервые.html>впервы́е</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpervýje</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>for the first time
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> колла́йдере <b><a href = vnd.unilang:впервые.html>впервы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:столкнуться.html>столкну́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:протон.html>прото́ны</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V kollájdɛre <b>vpervýje</b> stolknúlisʹ protóny.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In the collider protons were bashed together <b>for the first time</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a> (511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vperjód</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>forward
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>Вперёд</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берлин.html>берли́н</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vperjód</b> na Berlín!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Forward</b>, to Berlin!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> from now on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>Вперёд</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:незнакомый.html>незнако́мым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доверять.html>доверя́ть</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vperjód</b> búdešʹ znatʹ, kak neznakómym doverjátʹ!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>From now on</b>, you'll know how much trust to put in strangers!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>in advance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:платить.html>плати́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Platíte dénʹgi <b>vperjód</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Please pay <b>in advance</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">въ переди</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭ peredi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the latter the locative case of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">передь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which was displaced by modern <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перёд</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perjód</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">передъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***впечатление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ние</a> (1102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">впечатли́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpečatlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Eindruck</i>, which in turn is a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">impression</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpečatlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>impression
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ние</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:влюбиться.html>влюби́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>vpečatlénije</b>, što oní vljubílisʹ v drug drúga.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm under the impression that they've fallen in love with each other.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатлять.html>впечатля́ть</a> (17340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">впечатл-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpečatl-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатлять.html>впечатля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpečatljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">впечатли́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to impress
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатлять.html>впечатля́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto <b>vpečatljájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it's impressive (enough)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***впиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a> (13638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(into)</i>, to pierce, to bite <i>(into)</i>, to drive one's sting <i>(into)</i>, to dig one's fangs <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуба́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpivátʹsja</b> zubámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's teeth (into)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>когтя́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpivátʹsja</b> kogtjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's claws (into)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fix one's eyes <i>(on)</i>, to fix with one's eyes, to fasten one's eyes <i>(upon)</i>, to glue one's eyes <i>(to)</i></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>впи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-впи-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вписать.html>вписа́ть</a> (10520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписать.html>вписа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписывать.html>впи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enter, to insert <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something to the text that is already written by writing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to record <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something in a diary or a journal</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to inscribe</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вписаться.html>вписа́ться</a> (19336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписать.html>вписа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписаться.html>вписа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpisátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписываться.html>впи́сываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blend <i>(with)</i>, to fall in <i>(with)</i>, to fit <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вписаться.html>вписа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поворот.html>поворо́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>vpisátʹsja</b> v povorót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fail to follow the road bend (when driving)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fit <i>(into)</i>, to fit in <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вписаться.html>вписа́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коллектив.html>коллекти́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná ne <b>vpisálasʹ</b> v kollektív</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she didn't fit in with her colleagues</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписать.html>вписа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вписываться.html>впи́сываться</a> (14537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписывать.html>впи́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpísyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписываться.html>впи́сываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpísyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписаться.html>вписа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blend <i>(with)</i>, to fall in <i>(with)</i>, to fit <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to fit <i>(into)</i>, to fit in <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вписываться.html>впи́сывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto ne <b>vpísyvajetsja</b> v náši plány</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it doesn't agree [fit in] with our plans</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впитанный.html>впи́танный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpítannyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a> (8059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(into)</i>, to pierce, to bite <i>(into)</i>, to drive one's sting <i>(into)</i>, to dig one's fangs <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуба́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpítʹsja</b> zubámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's teeth (into)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>когтя́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpítʹsja</b> kogtjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's claws (into)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fix one's eyes <i>(on)</i>, to fix with one's eyes, to fasten one's eyes <i>(upon)</i>, to glue one's eyes <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>vpílsja</b> v nejó glazámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he couldn't take his eyes off her</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>впих<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — впихивать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-пих-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вползать.html>вполза́ть</a> (23370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вползти.html>вползти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpolztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вползать.html>вполза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpolzátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вползти.html>вползти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crawl in, to crawl inside</li>
<li>to crawl up, to climb up by crawling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to climb up with difficulty</li>
